//Created by libAntimony v2.0
function stepfunc2(t, t_start, v_start, t_end, v_end)
  piecewise(v_start, lt(t, t_start), v_end, gt(t, t_end), (v_end - v_start) / (t_end - t_start) * (t - t_start) + v_start);
end

function stepfunc(t, t_start, v_start, t_end, v_end)
  piecewise(v_start, lt(t, t_start), piecewise(v_end, gt(t, t_end), (v_start + v_end) / 2 + (v_end - v_start) / 2 * sin(3.14 / 2 * (2 * t - t_end - t_start) / (t_end - t_start))));
end
